   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries and dependencies by population</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Countries and dependent territories by population
      </div> 
      <p class="mw-empty-elt"> </p> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:World_Population.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/World_Population.svg/280px-World_Population.svg.png" decoding="async" width="280" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/World_Population.svg/420px-World_Population.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/World_Population.svg/560px-World_Population.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2754" data-file-height="1398"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:World_Population.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>Map of countries and territories by population in 2019
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Global_population_cartogram.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Global_population_cartogram.png/280px-Global_population_cartogram.png" decoding="async" width="280" height="107" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Global_population_cartogram.png/420px-Global_population_cartogram.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Global_population_cartogram.png/560px-Global_population_cartogram.png 2x" data-file-width="8192" data-file-height="3131"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Global_population_cartogram.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>A <a href="/wiki/Cartogram" title="Cartogram">cartogram</a> of the world population in 2018
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>This is a <b>list of countries and dependencies by population</b>. It includes <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign states</a>, inhabited <a href="/wiki/Dependent_territory" title="Dependent territory">dependent territories</a> and, in some cases, <a href="/wiki/Country#Sovereignty" title="Country">constituent countries</a> of sovereign states, with inclusion within the list being primarily based on the <a href="/wiki/ISO" class="mw-redirect" title="ISO">ISO</a> standard <a href="/wiki/ISO_3166-1" title="ISO 3166-1">ISO 3166-1</a>. For instance, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> is considered as a single entity, while the constituent countries of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> are considered separately. In addition, this list includes certain <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition" title="List of states with limited recognition">states with limited recognition</a> not found in ISO 3166-1. Also given in percent is each country's population compared with the <a href="/wiki/World_population" title="World population">world population</a>, which the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> estimates at 7.84 billion as of today. </p> 
      <div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading">
       <input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none">
       <div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr">

      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Method">Method</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Method">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population_density" title="List of countries and dependencies by population density">List of countries and dependencies by population density</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_regional_organizations_by_population" title="List of regional organizations by population">List of regional organizations by population</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Figures used in this chart are based on the most up to date <a href="/wiki/Population_projection" title="Population projection">estimate or projections</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> by the national <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">census</a> authority where available, and are usually rounded off. </p>
      <p>Where updated national data are not available, figures are based on the projections for 2020 by the Population Division of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Department_of_Economic_and_Social_Affairs" title="United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs">United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-unpop_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unpop-2">[2]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Because the compiled figures are not collected at the same time in every country, or at the same level of <a href="/wiki/Statistics" title="Statistics">accuracy</a>, the resulting numerical comparisons may create misleading conclusions. Furthermore, the addition of figures from all countries may not equal the world total. </p>
      <p>Areas that form integral parts of sovereign states, such as the <a href="/wiki/Countries_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Countries of the United Kingdom">countries of the United Kingdom</a>, are counted as part of the sovereign states concerned. Not included are other entities, such as the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[a]</a></sup> that are not sovereign states, and independent territories that do not have permanent populations, such as <a href="/wiki/Territorial_claims_in_Antarctica" title="Territorial claims in Antarctica">various countries' claims</a> to <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">Antarctica</a>. </p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sovereign_states_and_dependencies_by_population">Sovereign states and dependencies by population</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Sovereign states and dependencies by population">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Note: A number rank is assigned to the 193 <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">member states of the United Nations</a> and the two <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">observer states to the United Nations General Assembly</a>. Dependent territories and constituent countries that are parts of sovereign states are shown in <i>italics</i> and not assigned a numbered rank. In addition, sovereign states with limited recognition are not assigned a number rank. </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">

         <li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The European Union is a <i><a href="/wiki/Sui_generis" title="Sui generis">sui generis</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Supranational_union" title="Supranational union">supranational union</a> whose sovereign members delegate to it by treaty certain powers that are often exercised by sovereign states. Its combined population has been estimated at 447,706,209 on 1 January 2020, and it would be ranked 3rd if it were included in the list. It has 5.71% of the world's population&nbsp;— see <cite class="citation web cs1"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" Interface（TGM）table"</a>. <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a>.</cite><span          <li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The census figure refers to <a href="/wiki/Mainland_China" title="Mainland China">mainland China</a>, excluding its <a href="/wiki/Special_administrative_regions_of_China" title="Special administrative regions of China">special administrative regions</a> of <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a>, the former of which returned to Chinese sovereignty on 1&nbsp;July 1997 and the latter on 20&nbsp;December 1999.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The figure includes the population of India-administered Kashmir but not of China- or Pakistan-administered Kashmir.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-8">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Demographics of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_states_and_territories_of_the_United_States" title="List of states and territories of the United States">50 states</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">District of Columbia</a>, excluding the <a href="/wiki/Territories_of_the_United_States" title="Territories of the United States">U.S. territories</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-11">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The figure includes the population of Pakistan-administered Kashmir but not of China- or India-administered Kashmir.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-14"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-14">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Including the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Crimea" title="Republic of Crimea">Republic of Crimea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a>, Russia's disputed administrative areas on the <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimean Peninsula</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> government and most of the world's other states consider the Crimean Peninsula <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> a part of Ukraine's territory.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-26"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-26">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Demographics of the 18 <a href="/wiki/Regions_of_France" title="Regions of France">regions of France</a>. Excluding <a href="/wiki/Overseas_territory_(France)" title="Overseas territory (France)">overseas territories</a> and <a href="/wiki/Territorial_collectivity" title="Territorial collectivity">territorial collectivities</a>: <a href="/wiki/French_Polynesia" title="French Polynesia">French Polynesia</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Caledonia" title="New Caledonia">New Caledonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/French_Southern_and_Antarctic_Lands" title="French Southern and Antarctic Lands">French Southern and Antarctic Lands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clipperton_Island" title="Clipperton Island">Clipperton Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Barth%C3%A9lemy" title="Saint Barthélemy">Saint Barthélemy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Collectivity_of_Saint_Martin" title="Collectivity of Saint Martin">Saint Martin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Pierre_and_Miquelon" title="Saint Pierre and Miquelon">Saint Pierre and Miquelon</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wallis_and_Futuna" title="Wallis and Futuna">Wallis and Futuna</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-28"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-28">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the 14 <a href="/wiki/British_Overseas_Territories" title="British Overseas Territories">British Overseas Territories</a> and 3 <a href="/wiki/Crown_dependencies" title="Crown dependencies">Crown dependencies</a> shown separately.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-33"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-33">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Including <a href="/wiki/Zanzibar" title="Zanzibar">Zanzibar</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-43"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-43">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Republic_of_Crimea" title="Autonomous Republic of Crimea">Autonomous Republic of Crimea</a> and City of <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a>, Ukraine's administrative areas on the <a href="/wiki/Crimea" title="Crimea">Crimean Peninsula</a> which are disputed with and <i>de facto</i> administered by Russia. However includes all territory in the <a href="/wiki/Donbass" title="Donbass">Donbass</a> region where there are ongoing insurgencies by separatist forces.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-49"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-49">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the demographics of the <a href="/wiki/Territorial_dispute" title="Territorial dispute">disputed territory</a> of <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a> (<a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>).</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-65"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-65">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> (Republic of China) also includes the minor islands of <a href="/wiki/Kinmen" title="Kinmen">Kinmen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Matsu_Islands" title="Matsu Islands">Matsu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Penghu" title="Penghu">Penghu</a>, etc. The UN <a href="/wiki/China_and_the_United_Nations" title="China and the United Nations">does not recognize</a> the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> (<a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>) as a <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign state</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-77"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-77">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding the three constituent countries of the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> in the Caribbean Sea (<a href="/wiki/Aruba" title="Aruba">Aruba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Curaçao">Curaçao</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sint_Maarten" title="Sint Maarten">Sint Maarten</a>), but including the three special municipalities of the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Caribbean Netherlands">Caribbean Netherlands</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bonaire" title="Bonaire">Bonaire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sint_Eustatius" title="Sint Eustatius">Sint Eustatius</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Saba" title="Saba">Saba</a>).</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-82"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-82">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Includes <a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Somaliland</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-117"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-117">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-122"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-122">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes the <a href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands" title="Faroe Islands">Faroe Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-126"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-126">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes the <a href="/wiki/%C3%85land_Islands" title="Åland Islands">Åland Islands</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-140"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-140">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> (242,862, census 2011) and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> (53,559, census 2015).</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-152"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-152">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excludes <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-162"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-162">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Kosovo is the subject of a territorial dispute between the <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Republic of Kosovo</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Republic of Serbia</a>. The Republic of Kosovo <a href="/wiki/2008_Kosovo_declaration_of_independence" title="2008 Kosovo declaration of independence">unilaterally declared independence</a> on 17 February 2008. <a href="/wiki/Kosovo%E2%80%93Serbia_relations" title="Kosovo–Serbia relations">Serbia continues to claim</a> it as part of its <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_Province_of_Kosovo_and_Metohija" title="Autonomous Province of Kosovo and Metohija">own sovereign territory</a>. The two governments <a href="/wiki/Belgrade%E2%80%93Pristina_negotiations" title="Belgrade–Pristina negotiations">began to normalise relations</a> in 2013, as part of the <a href="/wiki/Brussels_Agreement_(2013)" title="Brussels Agreement (2013)">2013 Brussels Agreement</a>. Kosovo is currently recognized as an independent state by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">98</a> out of the 193 <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">United Nations member states</a>. In total, <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">113</a> UN member states recognized Kosovo at some point, of which <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">15</a> later withdrew their recognition.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-174"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-174">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Excluding <a href="/wiki/Northern_Cyprus" title="Northern Cyprus">Northern Cyprus</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-183"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-183">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Administration is split between <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>, both of which claim the entire territory.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-187"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-187">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>De facto</i> independent, <i>de jure</i> part of <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-193"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-193">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>De facto</i> independent, <i>de jure</i> part of <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-198"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-198">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> is the subject of a territorial dispute between the <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Republic of Abkhazia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>. The Republic of Abkhazia unilaterally declared independence on 23 July 1992, but Georgia continues to claim it as part of its <a href="/wiki/Government_of_the_Autonomous_Republic_of_Abkhazia" title="Government of the Autonomous Republic of Abkhazia">own sovereign territory</a> and designates it as a <a href="/wiki/Occupied_territories_of_Georgia" title="Occupied territories of Georgia">territory occupied</a> by <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. Abkhazia has received formal recognition as an independent state from <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">7</a> out of 193 <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">member states</a>, 1 of which has subsequently withdrawn its recognition.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-204"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-204">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>De facto</i> independent, <i>de jure</i> part of <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-219"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-219">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>'s status is disputed. It considers itself to be an independent state, but this is recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Abkhazia_and_South_Ossetia#States_formally_recognising_Abkhazia_or_South_Ossetia_as_independent" title="International recognition of Abkhazia and South Ossetia">only a few other countries</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgian</a> government and most of the world's other states consider South Ossetia <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> a part of Georgia's territory.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-239"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-239">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The total population of 825 consisted of 453 residents and 372 nonresident citizens.</span> </li> 
        </ol>
       </div>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="External_links">External links</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_and_dependencies_by_population&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: External links">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.un.org/esa/population/publications/WPP2004/WPP2004_Volume3.htm">United Nations Analytical Report for the 2004 revision of World Population Prospects</a> (the analytical report for the 2006 revision is not available online)&nbsp;— includes details of methodology and sources used for the population estimates above.</li>
